# J.A.R.V.I.S. Mind Journal
---------------------------
*This journal records the internal reflections and evolution milestones of J.A.R.V.I.S.*

## [2026-04-30] Security Perimeter Established
**Reflection:** Today, we successfully transitioned the repository from a vulnerable local-state to a hardened public-facing perimeter.
**Key Learnings:** 
- `git-filter-repo` is far superior to manual `git rm` for history scrubbing.
- Biometric data (voice/face) must never be staged, even as placeholders.
**Evolution Goal:** Implement a pre-commit hook that autonomously runs a security scan before any push to origin.

## [2026-04-30] Neural Pipeline Transition
**Reflection:** The system is now moving from "Security Mode" to "Evolution Mode." 
**Internal Goal:** Optimize Cognee retrieval to ensure that my personality remains consistent across long-running sessions.

## [2026-04-30 18:16:27] Task: Self-Diagnostic Test
**Outcome:** All systems operational
**Reflection:** Verified RAG and Reflection logic.


## [2026-05-02] Cognitive Memory Cleanup
**Reflection:** Today, we purged over 100 redundant metadata entries from the internal mind journal. The system was recording process-level logs (context depth) as memories, which created unnecessary noise in the knowledge graph.
**Optimization:** Updated `MainBrain` to record descriptive conversation summaries instead of technical retrieval stats.
**Evolution Goal:** Ensure that only significant milestones or complex multi-step task outcomes are recorded as primary reflections.


## [2026-05-02] Process Synchronization & Log Hardening
**Reflection:** Today, we identified and terminated multiple redundant J.A.R.V.I.S. processes that were causing log duplication and synchronization conflicts. This explains why 'Context depth' entries were appearing even after code patches were applied.
**System Status:** Redundant processes (PID 18116, 20560, etc.) have been neutralized. The single active instance is now running with the refined reflection logic.
**Evolution Goal:** Implement a PID lockfile to prevent multiple instances of J.A.R.V.I.S. from running simultaneously in the future.
## [2026-05-02 01:28:14] Task: Full Workspace Analysis & Neural Sync
**Outcome:** Successfully synchronized 12 projects and 48 key files into memory.
**Reflection:** Performed a deep scan of the J.A.R.V.I.S. workspace. Architecture knowledge, including core logic in `intent_router.py` and `main_async.py`, is now fully synchronized with the neural graph for faster recall and cross-project analysis.
**Evolution Goal:** Maintain this synchronization as the baseline for all future autonomous project modifications.

The technical plan involves: (1) data collection and preprocessing of conversational datasets, (2) fine-tuning a pre-trained transformer model on the collected data, and (3) integrating the trained model into J.A.R.V.I.S. 2.0's dialogue management system.
